# AutoTrading Change Ledger

This is the durable reason-and-outcome ledger for every material design, code, configuration, deployment, rollback, optimization, or live operational change.

## 2026-06-05 10:20 CST - Align A/v11 VPB funding queue wait with paced executor
- Trigger / reason: Post-cooldown staged restoration restarted API queue, market-data-cache, sentinel, then A/v11. Queue rows `955` and `956` showed mainnet public ticker requests returning `200` with no active cooldown. A/v11 then submitted a `strategy-breakout` public `premiumIndex` request to mainnet public, but the client waited only `timeout+5` seconds while the central executor is intentionally paced at `60s`; the request was cancelled as `client timeout cancelled queued request: queued` before execution. This was a local queue-wait mismatch, not a Binance `418/429/-1003`.
- Completed: Stopped A/v11 before continuing to B/C. Updated `strategy_breakout.py` so queue-backed VPB funding requests use the same default `BINANCE_API_QUEUE_CLIENT_TIMEOUT_SEC` wait as scanners, market-data-cache, and sentinel (`180s` default), while still allowing a larger explicit timeout. Strategy thresholds, scoring, sizing, leverage, stops, order/account endpoints, and Kline behavior are unchanged.
- Not completed / remaining: This restores the staged first-version service stack, not normal-universe expansion. A/B/C scanners still run with staged cache-only/public-market safeguards; long normal-universe observation, 30-day Kline/depth coverage, and natural open/close exact-case evidence remain post-launch backlog.
- Verification: `python -m py_compile 策略文件\strategy_breakout.py 策略文件\scanner.py` passed. `python -m unittest tests.test_binance_api_queue_client tests.test_kline_cache` passed (`10` tests). Pre-fix live queue check after stopping A showed `active_requests=[]`, `active_cooldowns=[]`, `max_rowid=957`, and no post-cooldown journal `HTTP 418/429/-1003`.
- Live impact / deployment: Live staged restoration actions: after the `10:06:50 CST` cooldown cleared, restarted `crypto-binance-api-queue.service`, then `crypto-market-data-cache.service`, then `crypto-market-mover-sentinel.service`, then A/B/C scanners one by one. No-restart A/v11 fix release `20260605-101709-strategy-a-e5b2638` was uploaded before A was restarted again. Final queue check showed `active_requests=[]`, `active_cooldowns=[]`, `max_rowid=967`; rows `960`, `963`, `964`, `967` were `strategy-breakout` mainnet public `premiumIndex` `200`, rows `955`, `958`, `961`, `965` were market-data-cache mainnet public ticker `200`, and rows `956`, `959`, `962`, `966` were sentinel mainnet public ticker `200`. Journal since `10:16 CST` had no `HTTP 418`, `HTTP 429`, `-1003`, `Traceback`, `ImportError`, `SyntaxError`, or fresh `client timeout`. Final `pull_live_context.py` at `10:29 CST` showed A/B/C scanners, sentinel, account-snapshot, and system-alerts active; positions `0`, upnl `0.0`, attention `P0=0/P1=0/P2=2`.
- Files / release / commit: `策略文件/strategy_breakout.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `记忆文档/MEMORY.md`; source commit `e5b2638`, deployment/restoration ledger follow-up pending.

## 2026-06-05 09:55 CST - Move scanner public market-data defaults off Testnet
- Trigger / reason: The 2026-06-05 recovery attempt showed Testnet public Kline can trigger `HTTP 418/-1003` even in a tiny staged run, and the follow-up source scan found the scanner/sentinel-adjacent public market-data paths still defaulted to Testnet for ticker, depth, funding, and premiumIndex style reads. These are public market-data inputs, not order/account endpoints, so they should not keep using the Testnet public host by default.
- Completed: A/v11, B/v16, C/v14 scanner market-data helper URLs now build from `BINANCE_MARKET_BASE_URL`, defaulting to Binance mainnet public `https://fapi.binance.com`. The market-data cache service uses the same configurable mainnet public default for `/fapi/v1/ticker/24hr`. A/v11 VPB funding reads in `strategy_breakout.py` also use `BINANCE_MARKET_BASE_URL` instead of hardcoded Testnet premiumIndex. Order/account/Testnet trading endpoints are unchanged.
- Not completed / remaining: This does not restart scanners/cache/sentinel or probe Binance during the active global cooldown. It also does not solve Kline history coverage by itself; scanners still need cache-only staged recovery, and longer Kline/depth coverage should come from controlled queue/backfill/ingest after post-cooldown checks are clean.
- Verification: `python -m py_compile 策略文件\market_data_service.py 策略文件\scanner.py 策略文件\scanner_v14.py 策略文件\scanner_v16.py 策略文件\strategy_breakout.py` passed. `python -m unittest tests.test_kline_cache tests.test_binance_api_queue_client tests.test_counterfactual_replay_fill` passed (`19` tests). `rg "testnet\.binancefuture\.com/fapi/v1/(klines|ticker|depth|fundingRate|premiumIndex|aggTrades|exchangeInfo)" .` returned no matches. `git diff --check` passed.
- Live impact / deployment: Pushed source commit `c0773e7` and deployed no-restart file uploads to Tencent: `20260605-095112-strategy-a-c0773e7`, `20260605-095156-strategy-b-c0773e7`, `20260605-095235-strategy-c-c0773e7`, and `20260605-095313-sentinel-c0773e7`. These uploads changed files on disk only; no service restart, queue executor start, scanner start, order/close, signed baseline, data reset, manual Binance probe, Kline/depth submit, or public market-data request occurred.
- Files / release / commit: `策略文件/market_data_service.py`, `策略文件/scanner.py`, `策略文件/scanner_v14.py`, `策略文件/scanner_v16.py`, `策略文件/strategy_breakout.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `PROJECT_STATE.md`, `记忆文档/MEMORY.md`, `记忆文档/FUTURE_EXECUTION_PLAN.md`; source commit `c0773e7`, deployment ledger follow-up pending.

## 2026-06-05 09:26 CST - Stop direct Testnet Kline fallback and switch scanner Kline source to mainnet public/cache
- Trigger / reason: User asked to continue full recovery while strictly avoiding Binance wind-control. A controlled A/v11 fresh-run after cooldown used BTCUSDT 15m Kline successfully, then ETHUSDT 15m Testnet Kline immediately hit `HTTP 418/-1003`; Binance reported IP ban until `2026-06-05 10:06:50 CST`. The old staged switch could still enable scanner direct Testnet Kline with only `SCANNER_KLINE_NETWORK_ENABLED=1`, so the same failure could recur on restoration.
- Completed: Stopped and contained the live failure before this code change: A/B/C scanners, market-data-cache, sentinel, and api-queue are inactive; the failed ETHUSDT Kline queue row was manually marked failed/no-retry; active queue requests are empty; user-stream, central-only account snapshot, and system alerts remain active. `core.kline_cache.kline_network_enabled()` now defaults off and requires both `SCANNER_KLINE_NETWORK_ENABLED=1` and `SCANNER_DIRECT_KLINE_NETWORK_ALLOWED=1`. A/B/C scanners now build Kline URLs through `kline_request_url()`, which defaults to Binance mainnet public `https://fapi.binance.com` instead of Testnet Kline if direct Kline networking is explicitly allowed later. `research_kline_backfill.py --submit` now writes an explicit mainnet public Kline URL into the central queue, so Kline backfill intent does not inherit the executor's Testnet base URL by accident.
- Not completed / remaining: No scanner/cache/sentinel/api-queue restart happened during the active global cooldown. Full staged recovery still waits for a read-only post-cooldown check after `2026-06-05 10:06:50 CST`; scanners must stay cache-only until a controlled Kline source/cache fill path is ready. Normal scanner universe, long observation, and 30-day Kline/depth coverage remain post-launch expansion.
- Verification: `python 部署工具\pull_live_context.py --logs-days 1 --log-tail 1200` showed positions `0`, upnl `0.0`, scanner/cache/sentinel inactive, account-snapshot/system-alerts active. ## 2026-06-05 00:10 CST - Simplify decision confirmations and add safe manual report refresh
- Trigger / reason: User asked whether `你需要确认的事项` was showing previous data, said the English experiment IDs and recommended actions were hard to understand, and asked whether the report should have a manual refresh button. Inspection showed the first-screen confirmation area was mixing old `cleared_pending_review` items and P2 observation strategy-evolution items with raw experiment IDs, even though the active Aliyun attention source currently has no open P0/P1.
- Completed: `decision_portal.py` now filters the first-screen confirmation table to only open P0/P1 items, keeps P2 observation items out of `你需要确认的事项`, and renders strategy/evolution/rollback items in plain Chinese wording instead of raw `EXP-*` / action-code text. Added a `刷新报表` button that calls the same-origin `/api/report/refresh` endpoint. `attention_api_server.py` now supports `GET/POST /api/report/refresh` with a single background refresh lock and runs the existing Aliyun lightweight `aliyun_decision_portal_refresh.sh` path when available. That path is report-only: bounded Tencent mirror sync, attention/skeleton/report regeneration, and reverse sync; it does not submit Binance queue work, run scanners, run account baselines, or call Binance REST. If the script is unavailable, the fallback only regenerates the local portal.
- Not completed / remaining: The report is still first-version operator UI; deeper visual polish and richer plain-language drilldown remain post-launch optimization. A post-deploy `pull_live_context.py` attempt could not complete because Tencent SSH timed out (`server 129.226.151.144 not responding`), so this entry does not claim a fresh Tencent live-context pull.
- Verification: `python -B -m py_compile 部署工具\decision_portal.py 部署工具\attention_api_server.py tests\test_decision_portal.py tests\test_attention_api_server.py` passed. `python -B -m unittest tests.test_attention_api_server tests.test_decision_portal` passed (`8` tests). `python -B 部署工具\decision_portal.py --out-dir reports` generated the local report; `reports/index.html` contains `刷新报表`, `/api/report/refresh`, and `暂无需要你确认的 P0/P1 事项`, while `EXP-*` is absent from the first-screen confirmation section for the current data. `git diff --check` passed with only CRLF warnings. `python 部署工具\git_change_guard.py` passed before the source commit. Public Aliyun checks after deployment returned `200` for `/api/health`; `GET /api/report/refresh` returned idle with `ok=true`, `mode=script`, and `safety=report_only_no_binance_submit`; `POST /api/report/refresh` started and completed the safe script refresh from `00:13:20` to `00:14:50 CST`; the public homepage now contains `刷新报表`, `/api/report/refresh`, and `暂无需要你确认的 P0/P1 事项`, with no `EXP-*` in the first-screen confirmation section.

The manual refresh invoked the lightweight Aliyun report-refresh script only. No Tencent trading service restart, no strategy threshold/stop/sizing change, no order/close, no signed baseline, no scanner start, no Kline/depth queue submit, no data reset, and no manual Binance probe.

## 2026-06-04 19:40 CST - Block staged scanner market-data fallback
- Trigger / reason: During post-launch staged restoration, a stale queued A/v11 public ticker row appeared even though scanners were supposed to run in cache-only staged mode. The remaining risk was that `fetch_top_symbols()` / `fetch_available_symbols()` / A/v11 volume-spike logic would fall back to `/fapi/v1/ticker/24hr` whenever `runtime/market_data_cache.json` was absent, stale, or incomplete.
- Completed: Added `market_data_network_enabled()` in `core.market_data_cache`. A/v11 volume-spike detection also stays local in this mode.

## 2026-06-04 02:40 CST - Add queued Kline backfill planner
- Trigger / reason: Continue offline-first long-term P1-E research warehouse work. Kline coverage acceptance can now report missing 30-day windows, but the system still needed a safe way to plan, queue, and later ingest historical Kline backfill without direct ad hoc Binance calls from analysis scripts.
- Completed: Added `research_kline_backfill.py` with three explicit modes: default plan-only mode reads existing `research_store/klines` and symbol seeds from `events` / `sentinel_scans`, `--submit` writes public `/fapi/v1/klines` intents into the central `BinanceApiQueue` with deterministic idempotency keys, and `--ingest-done` merges completed queued Kline results back into `research_store/klines` / `features` using the existing Kline feature exporter. It writes `runtime/research_kline_backfill_latest.json` and `reports/research_kline_backfill_latest.md`. Unit tests cover chunk planning, covered-interval skips, event-seeded planning when Klines are empty, queue-only submit, and DONE-result ingest.

Real historical Kline filling still needs a staged run using `--submit` under the central API queue, executor cooldown/backlog controls, `--ingest-done` after DONE results, and final `kline_acceptance=ok` on real post-refresh `15m/30m/1h` 30-day coverage. Long-history depth warehouse and retention/compression policy remain open.

## 2026-06-04 01:45 CST - Add depth-aware replay entry fill primitive
- Trigger / reason: Continue offline-first long-term P1-C replay/fill work. Partial-fill caps and fill-ratio sensitivity could approximate limited liquidity, but the shared fill kernel still lacked a first order-book-level entry simulation primitive.
- Completed: `core.replay_fill` now accepts optional `entry_order_book` levels. When provided, long entries consume asks and short entries consume bids, sorted by executable price, and compute average entry price, filled quantity, unfilled quantity, fill ratio, levels used, entry fill source, and depth slippage. Thin books can produce partial fills; strict no-partial replay fails closed. Explicit empty books now return `order book has no fillable liquidity` instead of silently using synthetic entry. Default behavior remains unchanged when no order book is supplied. Unit tests cover long asks, short bids, thin-book partials, strict partial rejection, and explicit empty-book failure.
- Not completed / remaining: This is a kernel primitive only. It does not fetch or persist depth snapshots, does not model queue priority, cancel/replace, or market impact beyond visible levels, and is not yet wired into counterfactual/rollout/recovery reports with real depth data. Remaining P1-C work: depth snapshot source, long-history Kline windows, and governance before replay/fill evidence can drive automatic rules.

The evolution gate had a single global P0/P1 sample threshold and fixed post-approval window maturity checks, but different strategy/change families carry different risk: A/v11 replacement, A/v11 trailing pullback, B/v16 exit-risk changes, C/v14 sample expansion, and confirmation-policy changes should not share one threshold.
- Completed: `strategy_evolution_gate.py` now selects a report-only `gate_profile` by strategy, change type, and candidate id. Profiles define P0/P1 minimum samples, 24h/72h/168h closed-sample requirements, and cross-regime robustness requirements. `classify_decision()`, `classify_window_quality()`, decision packets, per-decision payloads, and the Phase 8 hardening audit now use/expose these profile thresholds. The gate also adds a report-only `regime_robustness` score/status (`missing`, `single_regime`, `weak`, `ok`) using post-approval regime labels, ready windows, mature windows, and quality labels; the audit now reports profile counts, robustness status counts, and robustness gaps. Unit tests cover profile selection, 72h profile maturity, P1-vs-P0 sample boundary, regime robustness scoring, decision-packet output, and audit gaps.
- Not completed / remaining: This is still evidence and review gating only. It does not enable automatic upgrade or rollback, does not run full paper fill/slippage simulation with order-book depth or partial fills, and does not implement an operator-approved automatic rollback plan. Remaining P1-D work: fuller bar-by-bar/depth-aware paper fill/slippage simulation and rollback-plan governance; P0-A/P0-B final staged fresh-run remains required after offline work.

## 2026-06-03 18:50 CST - Add replay/live exact parity audit
- Trigger / reason: Continue offline-first long-term P0-B. The existing replay gate audit classified observed live rows, but it could still be confused with true same-input replay/live parity. The project needed a stricter audit that only counts serialized `strategy_gate_case(s)` evaluated through the real shared pure gates, while surfacing rows that still lack exact cases as coverage gaps.
- Completed: Added read-only `replay_live_parity_audit.py`. It reads recent `SIGNAL` / `OPEN` / `OPEN_SKIPPED` / `OPEN_FAILED` rows from SQLite, extracts nested `strategy_gate_case`, `gate_case`, or `parity_case` payloads, evaluates them through `core.strategy_gate_cases.evaluate_strategy_gate_case()`, and writes `runtime/replay_live_parity_latest.json` plus `reports/replay_live_parity_latest.md`. `portal_dashboard.py` now shows a function card, executive bullet/action, and a dedicated `Replay/live 同输入审计` section with exact-case coverage, pass rate, mismatches, errors, and top gates. Aliyun refresh/shadow scripts run the audit after replay gate audit; release bundles ship it; reverse sync and live-context pull include the new artifacts. ## 2026-06-03 11:05 CST - Add API queue pending-backlog fail-closed guard
- Trigger / reason: User redirected the work to offline-first construction before further server fresh-runs. The latest staged run showed the 60s queue executor can be overloaded by multiple public producers, producing queued/deferred buildup, timeout cancellations, and late replay risk.
- Completed: Added `BinanceApiQueue.pending_count()` and a queue-client pending backlog precheck. `queued_api_request()` now checks active cooldown first, then checks per-scope pending count before inserting a new request. Defaults are conservative but adjustable: public max pending `3`, signed max pending `20`, other scope max pending `10`, with per-scope env overrides and per-call `max_pending_requests`. ## 2026-06-02 22:58 CST - Add post-ban REST recovery ramp
- Trigger / reason: Natural post-cooldown verification at `22:31 CST` hit another public REST `418/-1003` from `public:C/v14 GET /fapi/v1/klines` after very low local request counts. Guard evidence showed several services waking together as the cooldown expired: account snapshot A balance/positionRisk, market-data-cache ticker, B/v16 ticker, C/v14 ticker/Klines, and sentinel ticker. This means simple per-minute limits are not enough during Binance/Testnet IP-ban recovery.
- Completed: `core/binance_api_guard.py` now has a post-ban recovery mode shared by signed and public REST callers. After `banned_until_ms`, all callers first observe `BINANCE_API_GUARD_POST_BAN_QUIET_MS` (default `5min`), then spend `BINANCE_API_GUARD_RECOVERY_WINDOW_MS` (default `30min`) in a combined signed+public ramp limited by default to `4/min` with `15000ms` minimum interval. The guard records `recovery_phase`, `post_ban_quiet_until_ms`, `recovery_until_ms`, and combined recovery rolling counts. `current_cooldown_seconds()` now includes the quiet period so account snapshots do not immediately resume at ban expiry. Added `tests/test_binance_api_guard.py`.
- Not completed / remaining: A `22:48:05 CST` public `418` occurred during the rollout window before all services had loaded the new guard, extending cooldown to `23:12:59`. Full verification must wait for the new cooldown plus the post-ban quiet/recovery window. P0-A still ultimately needs user-data-stream/central account-state and an independent queue/state service.
- Verification: `python -m unittest tests.test_binance_api_guard tests.test_strategy_gates` passed. Source compile-without-pycache passed for `core/binance_api_guard.py`, both test modules, account snapshot service, A/B/C scanners, sentinel, market-data-cache, and `release_manager.py`; `git diff --check` passed. ## 2026-06-02 19:38 CST - Space account snapshot collection and clear API P0
- Trigger / reason: After the 19:14 cooldown expired, the natural account snapshot cycle collected A/B successfully but hit Binance/Testnet `418/-1003` on `C/v14 GET /fapi/v2/balance` after five signed reads in the same burst. This proved scanners were no longer the source, but account snapshot still needed per-account pacing.
- Completed: `account_snapshot_service.py` now sleeps between successful account collections (`ACCOUNT_SNAPSHOT_ACCOUNT_GAP_SEC`, default `65s`) and checks the shared guard before each account. If a guard cooldown is active before an account, remaining accounts are filled from the last SQLite snapshot and no further signed requests are sent. If an account returns `418/429/-1003`, remaining accounts are also filled from the last snapshot and the cycle stops. `system_alerts.py` now downgrades historical API-limit journal lines to `warn` when the ban window has passed and the shared guard is no longer in cooldown, so stale 30-minute evidence does not keep a false P0 open after recovery.
- Not completed / remaining: This is still a REST pacing mitigation, not user-data-stream or a true central account-state service. Public REST is still at the `60/min` ceiling during scan bursts and should be watched for new 429s.
- Verification: Local `py_compile` passed for `account_snapshot_service.py` and `system_alerts.py`; `git diff --check` passed. Tencent account deploy `20260602-192150-account-a382614` succeeded; service restarted and logged `status=cooldown` rather than sending requests during the active guard cooldown. After cooldown expired, the next natural cycle completed at `2026-06-02T19:29:00+08:00` with `fresh_accounts=3`, `stale_accounts=[]`, `partial_error_count=0`, account upnl `+69.0386`, and `7` positions. Journal since `19:28:59` showed no new `418/429/-1003`. Guard at `19:37:57` showed `cooldown_seconds=0`, signed rolling `2`, public rolling `60/60`. ## 2026-06-02 01:18 CST - Add Binance API guard trade-priority reserve
- Trigger / reason: Continue the API-limit work after reducing duplicate scanner and A/v11 account reads. The remaining guard plan called for a priority path so non-trade reads cannot consume the whole rolling REST budget and delay order/close/cancel requests. Live context before this change showed all six services active and no 418/429 events, but `last_status=400` in the guard was also stale because successful requests did not clear the previous error marker.
- Completed: Updated `core/binance_api_guard.py` with request priority classification. `POST`/`DELETE` and trade-control endpoints such as order, leverage, margin type, and cancel-all are classified as `trade`; other signed reads are `normal`. The guard now reserves `BINANCE_API_GUARD_TRADE_PRIORITY_RESERVE_PER_MIN` slots, default `20/min`, so normal requests pause at `max_requests_per_min - reserve` while trade requests can use the reserved headroom up to the hard budget. It also clears stale `last_status` on new requests and stores error details under `last_error_*`. Updated `system_alerts.py` to expose `last_priority`, `last_error_*`, `rolling_limited_priority`, priority counts, normal limit, and trade reserve.

## 2026-06-01 21:22 CST - Add rolling Binance REST budget
- Trigger / reason: Continue the Binance API pressure work. The first API guard version persisted lifetime top paths and a global minimum interval, but it did not enforce a rolling request budget. A testnet IP ban is usually driven by burst pressure, so the guard needs a bounded 60-second budget.
- Completed: Extended `core/binance_api_guard.py` with `BINANCE_API_GUARD_MAX_REQUESTS_PER_MIN`, default `120`. The guard now keeps a bounded `recent_requests` window, writes `rolling_count_60s` and `max_requests_per_min`, and sleeps until the oldest request leaves the 60-second window when the process group reaches budget. `system_alerts.py` now exposes `top_paths_60s` in addition to lifetime top paths.
- Not completed / remaining: This still uses cooperative process-level waiting, not a true priority queue. Future work should separate trade-critical requests from reporting/snapshot requests, and should move account state to user-data-stream to reduce the need for signed REST in the first place.

## 2026-06-01 21:02 CST - Add cross-process Binance REST guard
- Trigger / reason: Continue the remaining medium/long-term plan with server pressure and Binance API limits as the highest priority. The live system had already raised account snapshot intervals and preserved snapshots on 418 errors, but A/v11, B/v16, C/v14, and the account snapshot service still made signed Binance REST calls from separate processes without a shared file-level throttle/cooldown state.

The guard enforces a configurable minimum inter-request interval across processes, persists `banned_until_ms` from `418/429/-1003/too many requests` responses, and makes sibling processes back off during the ban/cooldown window. Added the guard to `CORE_FILES` in `release_manager.py` so future strategy/account deploys always include it. ## 2026-06-01 16:34 CST - Make account snapshots resilient to one-account API failures
- Trigger / reason: Live report recovered the strategy-running card, but current-state pull still showed a P1 attention item: account snapshots were in Binance 418 cooldown and the last valid snapshot was more than two hours old. The account snapshot collector could fail the whole three-account snapshot when A/v11 hit a balance/position API error, making B/v16 and C/v14 disappear from fresh account reporting too.
- Completed: Updated `account_snapshot_service.py` to collect accounts independently. If one account fails, it falls back to that account's last SQLite `account_snapshots` payload, marks it `stale`, preserves the API error/cooldown record, and still writes fresh rows for accounts that succeeded. Updated `account_snapshot_html.py` to mark stale/fallback accounts visibly as `快照回退` instead of silently presenting them as normal. The service no longer inserts stale fallback rows into SQLite as fresh data.
- Not completed / remaining: This is a robustness fix for account snapshot/reporting. It does not solve Binance REST pressure permanently; the larger API-budget/user-data-stream migration remains future work before further scanner cadence expansion.
- Verification: Local `py_compile` passed for account snapshot service/html and portal. Tencent remote `py_compile` passed after deploy. ## 2026-05-31 23:46 CST - Add post-approval window quality thresholds
- Trigger / reason: Continue N4. Approved live candidates had post-approval windows and regime labels, but the gate still needed explicit window-quality thresholds for fee-adjusted loss, forced-close rate, and open-failure rate.

It estimates fee/slippage using 0.15% on 400 USDT notional per closed trade, computes `realized_pnl_after_cost`, forced-close rate, open-failure rate, and closed sample count. ## Recording Rule

- Update this file in the same commit as any material repository change.
- Record a live deploy, rollback, service/config change, or risk decision even when no source code changed.
- Keep generated runtime/log/report data out of Git; record only the conclusion, validation result, release id, and remaining work here.
- Update `PROJECT_STATE.md` when the current architecture, operating procedure, or open priorities change.
- Update `记忆文档/MEMORY.md` when a durable decision, important incident, or milestone should survive daily report rollover.
- Read-only inspection that yields no new decision, incident, or action does not require an empty Git commit.

## Entry Template

```markdown
## YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM CST - Short title
- Trigger / reason:
- Completed:
- Not completed / remaining:
- Verification:
- Live impact / deployment:
- Files / release / commit:
```
